### D-amplify-apex-spa-rewrite-deep-path-404-2026-05-20
**Status:** OPEN — P3 (deferred low-priority infrastructure-config drift). Surfaced 2026-05-20 during the Step 30a.7 diligence-pass validation probes against the `step-30a-7-diligence` arc closure on Pricing.tsx (Amplify build #27, commit `d41bc232`). When probing the live Pricing page, `curl https://vantagemind.ai/pricing` returned HTTP 404 (Amplify default "Not Found" page, 143 bytes) while `curl https://www.vantagemind.ai/pricing` returned HTTP 200 (SPA shell, 1,640 bytes, hydrates correctly). The apex→www redirect works at the root (`https://vantagemind.ai/` → 301 → `https://www.vantagemind.ai/`) but does not catch deep paths on the apex hostname.
**Section that raised it:** Step 30a.7 diligence-pass post-deploy validation, 2026-05-20 ≈14:48 EDT. Surfaced as a side-discovery during the `D-pricing-cards-eighteen-dimension-matrix-surface-2026-05-20` closure-evidence probe.
**Raised by:** Agent during live-validation probe, 2026-05-20 post-build-#27.
**Design claim:** A user typing `vantagemind.ai/pricing` (apex without `www`, deep path) should reach the live Pricing page, either by (a) issuing a 301 to `www.vantagemind.ai/pricing` that preserves the deep path, or (b) by the apex hostname carrying its own SPA-fallback rewrite rule that maps any non-asset path to `/index.html` (so the React Router resolves `/pricing` client-side). Either configuration is acceptable; the current state — apex deep-path returns 404, www deep-path returns 200 — is asymmetric and represents an Amplify rewrite-rule gap on the apex domain entry.
**Repo state:** No repository artifact — this is pure Amplify console configuration (App `d1xf2f9605mosw`, domain settings + rewrite rules). The Amplify rewrite rule that maps `/<*>` → `/index.html` (200) for SPA fallback is presumably scoped to the `www` subdomain hostname only; the apex hostname either lacks the SPA-fallback rule entirely or has it configured but masked by an earlier redirect rule that doesn't preserve the path.
**Operational impact today:** Low. Apex deep-path 404 affects only the narrow surface of users who manually type `vantagemind.ai/pricing` (or any deep path) into the address bar without the `www`. The majority of organic traffic (a) lands on apex `/` first (which redirects to www cleanly) before navigating to `/pricing` via the in-page nav, (b) arrives via in-marketing links that already carry the `www` prefix, or (c) arrives via search-engine results pages where Google's canonical form will be the www variant. No customer impact has been reported. The break-glass workaround is the apex root redirect, which still works.
**Owning roadmap step:** Deferred to next Amplify infrastructure-config touch (no dedicated step). The fix is a two-line Amplify console rewrite-rule addition on the apex hostname: `/<*>` → `https://www.vantagemind.ai/<*>` (301, path-preserving) — or alternately, an SPA-fallback rule `/<*>` → `/index.html` (200) on the apex hostname matching what www carries. Either is acceptable; the path-preserving 301 is preferred because it concentrates traffic on a single canonical hostname for SEO and analytics purposes.
**Resolution path:**

1. Operator opens Amplify console for app `d1xf2f9605mosw`, navigates to Domain management → `vantagemind.ai` apex configuration.
2. Add rewrite rule: source `/<*>`, target `https://www.vantagemind.ai/<*>`, type `301 (Permanent redirect)` — ensure rule ordering places this AFTER any explicit asset-path rules and BEFORE the catch-all fallback.
3. Verify with `curl -I https://vantagemind.ai/pricing` → expect `HTTP/2 301` with `location: https://www.vantagemind.ai/pricing` header; `curl -sL https://vantagemind.ai/pricing | wc -c` → expect ≥1640 bytes (the SPA shell, not the 143-byte 404 page).
4. On verification, close drift with strikethrough in §3, append closure stanza in §5 with the `curl -I` evidence captured pre-fix and post-fix.

**Pattern E:** Infrastructure-config drift, no code change. No risk to the website surface itself; the React Router and Pricing.tsx are unaffected. The fix is entirely in the Amplify console domain-rewrite configuration. P3 priority is appropriate because (a) the most-visited entry path (apex root) works, (b) no customer impact has been reported, (c) the fix is a console-level change rather than a code-and-build cycle, and (d) the validation-probe asymmetry doesn't block any in-flight customer journey.
**Validation evidence (today, pre-fix):** `curl -sSL --max-time 15 -H "Accept: text/html" -o /tmp/pricing2.html -w "HTTP %{http_code}, %{size_download} bytes\n" https://vantagemind.ai/pricing` → `HTTP 404, 143 bytes`; response body is the Amplify default 404 page (`<title>Not Found</title>`). Compare against `curl -sSL --max-time 15 -o /tmp/pricing-www.html -w "HTTP %{http_code}, %{size_download} bytes\n" https://www.vantagemind.ai/pricing` → `HTTP 200, 1640 bytes` (SPA shell, hydrates correctly). Captured 2026-05-20 ≈14:48 EDT post-Amplify-build-#27.
**Cross-refs:** `~~D-pricing-cards-eighteen-dimension-matrix-surface-2026-05-20~~` (parent: this drift surfaced during the validation probes of that closure); `D-pricing-page-truth-2026-05-20` (sibling Pricing-surface umbrella, indirect — apex 404 affects the Pricing-page truth surface from the apex hostname); Amplify app `d1xf2f9605mosw` domain configuration (the fix-target artifact, not a repo file).

### D-entitlement-matrix-v1-roadmap-rows-deferred-2026-05-20
**Status:** OPEN — P1 umbrella carve-out for the eight Roadmap-classed rows of the Step 30a.6 entitlement matrix v1. Surfaced 2026-05-20 at Step 30a.6 Pass 2, when the entitlement matrix authored in CANONICAL_RECAP §14 split each cell into a **Live-Today** value (enforced at runtime today) and a **Roadmap** value (committed to the buyer, enforcement deferred to a named follow-up Step). The eight Roadmap rows are carried under this single umbrella rather than as eight separate stub drifts (per Aryan's 2026-05-20 "I will entrust you with the judgements partner" lock) — the per-row drift opens lazily at the corresponding-Step touch, so the eight stubs do not pollute §3 ahead of any actual enforcement work. The buyer-facing matrix is truthful from day one because every Roadmap cell is labelled as such on Pricing.tsx and in §14; what this drift records is the operational deferral, not a deception.
**Section that raised it:** CANONICAL_RECAP §14 "Entitlement matrix" sub-section authored 2026-05-20 at Step 30a.6 Pass 2; sibling to `D-entitlement-matrix-v1-2026-05-20` (which carries the policy-module half of the same step).
**Raised by:** Agent at Step 30a.6 Pass 2 close, on the 2026-05-20 partner direction "I will entrust you with the judgements partner" (on carve-out drift shape) and "Update our roadmap as necessary you are well aware of our and the discipline and symmetery we try to main" (on preserving §3 discipline without 2hr of near-identical stubs).
**Design claim:** The entitlement matrix v1 in CANONICAL_RECAP §14 is authored against three tiers × 18 dimensions, with each cell carrying either a Live-Today enforcement (in `app/policy/entitlements.py` + the wiring to its existing service-layer call-site) or a Roadmap enforcement (declared in the policy module, gated on a named follow-up Step). The policy module is the operational source of truth; the §14 table is the buyer-facing surface of the same shape; the two cannot drift apart.
**Repo state:** At Pass 2 close, `app/policy/entitlements.py` has not yet been authored (Pass 3 deliverable). The 18 dimensions are enumerated only in CANONICAL_RECAP §14. The eight Roadmap rows carried under this umbrella are:

| # | Dimension | Pairing Step | Enforcement target | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 9 | Conversations per day, per seat | Step 34 (workflow actions) + Step 31.x (per-seat metering) | Per-seat counter on inbound chat turn; cap value resolved from `ENTITLEMENTS_BY_TIER[<tier>].conversations_per_day_per_seat`; fail-open soft warning at 80%, fail-closed at 100% | Counter not built; deferred at Step 30a.6 |
| 10 | API rate limit (requests per minute, per tenant) | Step 31.x (rate-limit profiles) | `RateLimitFallback` middleware extension to resolve the per-minute cap from tier rather than the current uniform value | Per-tier profile not wired; deferred at Step 30a.6 |
| 11 | Concurrent Sarah instances | Step 36 (Luciel Council) + Step 31.x | Concurrency counter on LLM dispatch; cap resolved from `ENTITLEMENTS_BY_TIER[<tier>].concurrent_sarah_instances` | Counter not built; deferred at Step 30a.6 |
| 12 | Cross-domain memory (Company-only) | Step 37 (hybrid retrieval) | Tier-gating of cross-Domain retrieval at the retriever layer; Step 24.5c primitives already present but tier-check not yet wired | Tier-gating not enforced; deferred at Step 30a.6 |
| 13 | Audit retention (30/90/365 days per tier) | Next cron touch (purge worker from Step 30a.2) | Per-tier retention class wired into the purge worker; currently tier-agnostic uniform 90-day window | Tier-agnostic today; deferred at Step 30a.6 |
| 14 | Audit CSV export (Company-only) | Step 31.x (audit-export surface) | New `/api/v1/audit/export` route gated on `ENTITLEMENTS_BY_TIER[<tier>].audit_csv_export`; no route exists today | No route; deferred at Step 30a.6 |
| 15 | Custom widget branding (Company-only) | Next widget surface touch | Tier-gating of who can set the widget theme field; Step 30b widget carries the theme field today but does not enforce per-tier write access | Field exists, gating absent; deferred at Step 30a.6 |
| 16 | SSO (Company-only, future enterprise) | Future enterprise step beyond Step 33b | SAML / OIDC integration surface; no integration today | No integration; deferred at Step 30a.6 |

(The four operator-process rows — Priority support tiers, Dedicated success manager, plus the three channel-adapter rows for Voice / SMS / Email — are also Roadmap-classed in §14, but Voice/SMS/Email are carried under the sibling drift `D-channels-promised-not-built-multi-tier-2026-05-20` (their pairing Step is Step 34a in one block), and the two support-process rows are operator-process commitments that do not need a code-side drift home. The eight rows above are the deferred-code rows that this umbrella carves out.)
**Operational impact today:** Zero customer-visible impact today, because no customer is on a Team or Company tier (the only Company-tier tenant, `co-354c5056`, is being retired in parallel with this Pass 2). Every Roadmap entitlement is labelled as such on Pricing.tsx and in CANONICAL_RECAP §14 "Entitlement matrix" sub-section, so the buyer surface remains truthful. The operational risk this carve-out manages is **drift-velocity risk**: if these eight rows are not tracked as a coherent block, individual rows can be quietly forgotten over the next 6–12 months as the codebase grows; the umbrella forces a status-table review on each follow-up Step touch.
**Owning roadmap step:** Step 30a.6 — entitlement matrix v1 (this drift's parent). Per-row enforcement lands at the pairing Step in the status table above. The umbrella resolves only when all eight Roadmap rows have either landed enforcement (per-row drift opens, closes, strikes through in §5) or been deliberately re-classified (e.g. SSO might be re-routed to Step 33b proper rather than a beyond-33b step, in which case the row's pairing-Step cell is annotated and the umbrella row stays).
**Resolution path:**

1. At Step 30a.6 Pass 3, `app/policy/entitlements.py` is authored with all 18 dimensions declared, each with a Live-Today value and a Roadmap value. The eight Roadmap rows above are declared with `enforced=False` and a `pairing_step` field naming the follow-up Step.
2. On each follow-up Step that lands enforcement for one or more of these rows, a per-row drift opens (e.g. at Step 34 the `D-conversations-per-day-per-seat-counter-missing-YYYY-MM-DD` drift opens, closes at that step's commit, strikes through in §5). The row's status cell above is updated from "deferred at Step 30a.6" to a strikethrough with the closing drift slug and date.
3. When all eight row-status cells above are strikethroughs, this umbrella moves to RESOLVED with its own closing date, and the strikethrough version preserves the full pre-closure body in §5 per §6 doctrine.

**Pattern E (Drift surfaced by partner pre-Journey-1 review, 2026-05-20):** Pattern E for design-truth gaps where the operational deferral is acknowledged-and-tracked rather than fixed-in-the-same-pass. The umbrella shape is the partner-approved compaction of what would otherwise be eight near-identical OPEN entries; the discipline is preserved by the status table inside the umbrella, which is required reading at every follow-up Step touch that lands one of the eight rows.
**Validation evidence:** None today (Pass 2 doc-truthing only; no code lands until Pass 3). The Pass 3 deliverable will include the `app/policy/entitlements.py` module with the 18 dimensions declared and the `pairing_step` field on each Roadmap row; validation will assert (in a unit test) that every row in the §14 table appears in the module and vice versa.

**Status:** RESOLVED on 2026-05-22 by the broader Arc 4 tenancy collapse. Implementation closure lands when the Arc 4 execution arc (`arc4-out/A-collapse-plan.md`) completes.
**Original Status (pre-closure):** OPEN — P0 design-truth + product-shape umbrella. Surfaced on 2026-05-20 during the partner-led pre-Journey-1 review of the live E2E_USER_STORIES surface, when Aryan stopped the resumed Step 30a.5 / Step 30a.4 / Step 30a Individual smoke walk before the first Stripe-Checkout card-entry to raise three concerns against the live tier model: (1) the public Pricing surface advertises trial copy and a Book-a-demo CTA that no longer match the paid-intro shape (`D-pricing-page-truth-2026-05-20`, `D-nav-demo-cta-replaced-with-login-2026-05-20`, `D-annual-cadence-two-months-free-framing-2026-05-20`); (2) the tier-hierarchy semantics inherited from the 2026-05-13 Step 30a.1 closure — "Team is `agent + domain` provisioning and Company is `agent + domain + tenant`" (CANONICAL_RECAP §12 Step 30a.1 row; §14 "Why the price difference is what it is") — bake a domain layer into Team that does not match the way a department actually buys (a small team is flat — one lead, N teammates, no sub-departments), and conflate Company's value driver (multiple Domains) with Team's value driver (cross-teammate memory under a single department); (3) the entitlement matrix that distinguishes the three tiers beyond instance cap and price has never been authored as a single first-class artifact (`D-entitlement-matrix-v1-2026-05-20`), so the price-difference defence in §14 is currently load-bearing on the Luciel-shape difference alone, with no operational rate-limit / conversation-cap / channel-availability / branding / SSO / SLA dimensions surfaced to the buyer or enforced in code. This umbrella drift records the realignment of the tier model itself; the five sibling drifts (this one + the four named above + `D-channels-promised-not-built-multi-tier-2026-05-20`) carry the per-surface execution.
**Section that raised it:** Pre-Journey-1 live-testing pause, 2026-05-20 ≈ partner's morning session, after the agent walked the resumed Step 30a.5 smoke through Pricing → Individual CTA → Stripe Checkout (`cs_live_b1dsWeu4fB5Dw2nOJkPVZXFaCCaKX2ramgER4ZfG6hQ4xElc6OthMKAsUx`, buyer `aryans.www+test-ind-may19@gmail.com`) and stopped at card entry to raise the three concerns. **Design claim:** CANONICAL_RECAP §14 commits that the three tiers exist as separate products — "A Team Luciel is not a bigger Individual Luciel. It can see across all the team's work, learn from all of their conversations, and act on behalf of any of them — that's a different product, and a different value, not a larger version of the same one. The same goes from Team to Company." CANONICAL_RECAP §12 Step 30a.1 closure operationalises that as "Team is `agent + domain` provisioning and Company is `agent + domain + tenant` — the price difference tracks a real product difference." ARCHITECTURE §4.1 (scope hierarchy as billing boundary) and §3.2.13 (Billing surface) jointly commit that every tier's hierarchy is reflected in the scope-bearing rows pre-minted at signup. The realignment claim being recorded today: the §14 product-difference story is correct, but the §12 Step 30a.1 operationalisation overshot — a Team tenant should be **flat** (`tenant → agents`, no Domain layer), not `tenant → 1 default domain → agents`. The Team product difference (cross-teammate memory under one department) is delivered by the cross-domain memory primitive Step 24.5c already lays down at the `conversation_id` level, not by a Domain-layer mint. Company stays two-level (`tenant → domains → agents`). This is a tightening of the product hierarchy, not an inversion.
**Repo state:** Defect distributed across two source files and three doc files. (a) `app/services/tier_provisioning_service.py` lines 242–264 (the "3. Team + Company tiers ALSO get the domain-scope Team Luciel" branch) currently mints a domain-scope `LucielInstance` under `DEFAULT_DOMAIN_ID` for both Team and Company; the Team branch must be removed, leaving a Team tenant with a single agent-scope `LucielInstance` and no domain-scope mint. (b) `app/models/subscription.py` line 139 — `DOMAIN_COUNT_CAP_BY_TIER = {TIER_INDIVIDUAL: 0, TIER_TEAM: 1, TIER_COMPANY: 50}` — Team flips from `1` to `0`; the Individual `0` and Company `50` rows are correct as-is. (c) `app/services/admin_service.py` `_enforce_tier_scope` — the tier→allowed-scope map currently allows Team to operate at `scope_level=domain`; must tighten to `agent` only for Team. (d) `app/services/invite_service.py` — invite-role policy must be authored as a per-tier role matrix: `team_admin` can only invite `agent`; `company_admin` can only invite `domain_admin`; `domain_admin` can only invite `agent`. (e) CANONICAL_RECAP §12 Step 30a.1 closure language ("Team is `agent + domain`") and §14 "Why the price difference is what it is" paragraph both need a surgical rewrite to record the realigned semantics. (f) ARCHITECTURE §3.2.13 and §4.1 ✅ markers on the Step 30a.1 / Step 30a.5 closures flip to 🔧 until the realignment lands. (g) E2E_USER_STORIES.md Team and Company sections need a full rewrite against the new hierarchy.
**Operational impact today:** Critical-but-narrow. One live tenant (`co-354c5056`, Company tier, $1,000 intro paid 2026-05-18) exists on the wire under the old semantics; its retirement is the precondition for the realignment landing cleanly on a clean slate. ### ~~D-pricing-page-truth-2026-05-20~~
**Status:** RESOLVED on 2026-05-20 by the Step 30a.6 + Step 30a.7 Pricing-surface arcs (commits `b78dc9d` Step 30a.6 + `8af13bb` Step 30a.7 catch-up + `d41bc23` Step 30a.7 diligence-pass) shipped via Amplify build #27 to `https://www.vantagemind.ai/pricing`. §3 strikethrough applied 2026-05-20 in the Arc 1 doc-hygiene sweep. **Original Status (pre-closure):** OPEN — P1 marketing-truth. The public Pricing surface at `https://www.vantagemind.ai/pricing` (source: `Luciel-Website/src/pages/Pricing.tsx`) advertises three claims that no longer match the live billing surface: (a) **trial copy** — the monthly cards carry "14-day free trial" (Individual) and "7-day free trial" (Team, Company) language, both of which were superseded by the paid-intro shape on 2026-05-14 (Step 30a.2 + per-tier scaling 2026-05-16 — see CANONICAL_RECAP §14 "Intro offer" paragraph); the live behaviour today is a one-time intro fee ($100 Individual / $300 Team / $1,000 Company) followed by a 90-day trial on the recurring price; (b) **"2 months free"** annual-cadence framing — the cards advertise annual as "2 months free per year" against a 10× monthly anchor, which is mathematically true but reads as a discount-framing that does not match the §14 stance (annual is one-bill-a-year for a different buyer profile, not a discount play); (c) **"Book a demo"** CTA on the Company card — the self-serve Company surface is live (Step 30a.5 closed 2026-05-18 with $1,000 paid evidence on tenant `co-354c5056`), so the Book-a-demo CTA undersells the product by routing the highest-tier buyer away from the live checkout into an operator-touch path that does not exist today. All three are marketing-truth defects, not customer-visible regressions, but each one is a load-bearing claim on the Pricing surface that a paying customer reads before they click Start.
**Section that raised it:** Pre-Journey-1 live-testing pause, 2026-05-20, during the partner walk of the live Pricing surface alongside the umbrella tier-realignment drift. Concern #1 in the partner's three-concern review.
**Raised by:** Aryan (partner) on 2026-05-20, in the same direction-setting message that paused Journey 1.
**Design claim:** CANONICAL_RECAP §14 commits the paid-intro shape as the live behaviour from 2026-05-14 onward and the per-tier scaling from 2026-05-16 onward. The §14 "Annual cadence shape" paragraph commits annual as one-bill-a-year (no trial, distinct from monthly), not as a discount play. CANONICAL_RECAP §12 Step 30a.5 closure commits Company as self-serve ($1,000 paid evidence on tenant `co-354c5056`). The Pricing surface is the customer-facing implementation of all three claims; the current copy is from the pre-Step-30a.2 era and has accumulated drift against three separate post-30a.2 design moves.
**Repo state:** Defect at `Luciel-Website/src/pages/Pricing.tsx` (file size 18483 bytes, last modified 2026-05-19 — last touched at the Step 30a.5 post-smoke commit on 2026-05-18 but not for the Pricing-copy surface). Specific copy strings to remove or replace: (a) the "14-day free trial" and "7-day free trial" lines on the Individual / Team / Company monthly cards — replaced by "$100 intro, then $30/mo" / "$300 intro, then $300/mo" / "$1,000 intro, then $2,000/mo" framing that matches the §14 per-tier intro language; (b) the "2 months free" line on each annual card — replaced by "One bill a year, $300 / $3,000 / $20,000 CAD" framing that matches the §14 "Annual cadence shape" stance; (c) the "Book a demo" CTA on the Company card — replaced by the same "Start with $1,000 intro" CTA the Individual and Team cards use, routing to the same Stripe Checkout surface (`POST /api/v1/billing/checkout` with `tier=company, cadence=monthly`).
**Operational impact today:** Low-but-load-bearing. The Pricing surface is the customer's first contact with the live billing claims; every mismatch between the surface and the live behaviour is a credibility cost at the moment of payment. The 2026-05-19 partner Journey 1 walk reached the Stripe Checkout page (`cs_live_b1dsWeu4fB5Dw2nOJkPVZXFaCCaKX2ramgER4ZfG6hQ4xElc6OthMKAsUx`) before noticing the mismatch — the buyer reads "14-day free trial" on Pricing, then sees the $100 line item on Stripe Checkout, and the cognitive dissonance is exactly the moment trust frays. No live customer has hit this path under the new intro shape because the only live tenant (`co-354c5056`) was Company-tier and paid the $1,000 intro through a different copy path; impact escalates the moment Individual or Team traffic actually clicks Start.
**Owning roadmap step:** Step 30a.6 (Tier-hierarchy realignment) closing tag, paired with the four sibling drifts. Pass 3 of the realignment commit arc.
**Resolution path:** Single-file edit at `Luciel-Website/src/pages/Pricing.tsx`. Three string-replacement passes: (a) remove every "X-day free trial" string, replace with the per-tier intro-fee + recurring-price framing; (b) remove every "2 months free" string, replace with the one-bill-a-year framing; (c) replace the Company-card "Book a demo" CTA element with the same Start CTA shape the Individual and Team cards use. Add three vitest cases at `Luciel-Website/src/pages/__tests__/Pricing.test.tsx` pinning the contract: the rendered Pricing surface contains no occurrence of the substring `"trial"` or `"2 months free"` or `"Book a demo"`, and contains exactly three Start CTAs.
**Pattern E:** Pure copy fix at the website-surface layer. No backend touch. No schema change. No route signature change. The Stripe Checkout surface the CTAs route to is unchanged. The three vitest cases are additive in the test suite.
**Validation evidence:** Pending. Discovery evidence is the 2026-05-20 partner walk against the live `https://www.vantagemind.ai/pricing` surface. ### ~~D-nav-demo-cta-replaced-with-login-2026-05-20~~
**Status:** RESOLVED on 2026-05-20 by the Step 30a.6 tier-hierarchy realignment commit (`b78dc9d` on `Luciel-Website`) shipped via Amplify build #27. §3 strikethrough applied 2026-05-20 in the Arc 1 doc-hygiene sweep. Closure stanza in §5 below.
**Original Status (pre-closure):** OPEN — P2 marketing-truth + customer-journey. The Luciel-Website global navigation (source: `Luciel-Website/src/components/Nav.tsx` or equivalent header component) carries a "Book a demo" CTA in the right-hand action slot, inherited from the pre-self-serve marketing era (Step 30a-pre, when Company traffic was operator-touch by default). With Step 30a.5 closed and a live $1,000 self-serve Company purchase on the wire, the Book-a-demo CTA is a stale affordance that routes existing customers away from the right action (logging into `/app`) and routes new buyers away from the right action (clicking Start on Pricing). The right action in the Nav slot today is **Login** — the surface that takes a paying customer from any marketing-site page directly to `/login`, where they type email + password (Step 30a.3 surface) and land on `/app` cookied.
**Section that raised it:** Pre-Journey-1 live-testing pause, 2026-05-20, during the partner walk of the live Nav surface alongside the umbrella tier-realignment drift. Sub-concern of Pricing-page truth (`D-pricing-page-truth-2026-05-20`), separated out as its own drift because the Nav surface is a distinct surface from the Pricing page surface — same defect class, different implementation file, different render context (Nav renders on every page; Pricing renders only at `/pricing`).
**Raised by:** Aryan (partner) on 2026-05-20, in the same direction-setting message.
**Design claim:** CANONICAL_RECAP §12 Step 30a.3 closure committed password authentication as mandatory at every signup across every tier, with `/login` as the daily-login surface for paying customers. The Nav surface is the implementation home for the always-reachable Login affordance; the current Nav presents Book-a-demo instead, which violates the implicit precondition that every paying customer can reach their workspace from every marketing-site page in one click.
**Repo state:** Defect at `Luciel-Website/src/components/Nav.tsx` (component file location to be verified at the resolution-commit pass — the website repo's component conventions place the Nav in `src/components/` or `src/layouts/`). Pre-fix, the Nav action slot renders a `<Link to="/contact?subject=demo">Book a demo</Link>` (or equivalent). Post-fix, the same slot renders `<Link to="/login">Login</Link>` — same styling, same position, different target and label.
**Operational impact today:** Low — the Nav Book-a-demo CTA does not block any flow (a paying customer can still reach `/login` by typing the URL, and a new buyer can still reach Pricing by clicking the Pricing nav-link). Impact is reputational: a paying customer who navigates back to the marketing site after their session expires sees Book-a-demo instead of Login, which reads as if the product does not yet have a workspace they can log into. Impact escalates if a paying customer mentions the Nav surface in a referral or screenshot — the Book-a-demo CTA actively undersells the live self-serve product.
**Owning roadmap step:** Step 30a.6 (Tier-hierarchy realignment) closing tag, paired with the four sibling drifts. Pass 3 of the realignment commit arc.
**Resolution path:** Single-component edit. (a) Locate the Nav component (likely `Luciel-Website/src/components/Nav.tsx` or `src/layouts/MarketingLayout.tsx`). (b) Replace the Book-a-demo action-slot element with a Login link pointing at `/login`. (c) Add one vitest case at `Luciel-Website/src/components/__tests__/Nav.test.tsx` (or extend an existing Nav test if present) pinning the contract: the rendered Nav contains a `<a>` with `href="/login"` and visible text `Login`, and contains no occurrence of the substring `Book a demo`.
**Pattern E:** Pure copy + link fix at the website-component layer. No backend touch. No schema change. No new route on the marketing site (the `/login` page already exists per Step 30a.3). No regression risk to the existing Pricing nav-link, Logo home-link, or any other Nav element.
**Validation evidence:** Pending. Discovery evidence is the 2026-05-20 partner walk against the live Nav surface (visible on every marketing-site page including `/pricing`). Closure evidence is (a) the vitest case green; (b) `Invoke-WebRequest https://www.vantagemind.ai/` post-deploy returns HTML whose Nav region contains a `Login` link and no `Book a demo` substring; (c) the resumed Journey 1 walk surfaces the Login affordance from the Nav on at least one intermediate page navigation.
**Cross-refs:** CANONICAL_RECAP §12 Step 30a.3 closure stanza (the password-auth + `/login` surface this drift defends); `D-tier-semantics-realignment-2026-05-20` (umbrella); `D-pricing-page-truth-2026-05-20` (sibling — the Pricing-card Book-a-demo CTA is removed in the same Pass 3 commit; the Nav Book-a-demo CTA is the second occurrence of the same defect class on the website surface); `D-marketing-product-boundary-soft-2026-05-16` (predecessor — the marketing-product-boundary drift carrying the broader "marketing surface is out of step with the product surface" pattern).

### ~~D-annual-cadence-two-months-free-framing-2026-05-20~~
**Status:** RESOLVED on 2026-05-20 (Step 30a.7 Pricing surface catch-up). Closure stanza in §5 below.
**Original status (preserved for audit):** OPEN — P3 marketing-framing. The §14 "Annual cadence shape" paragraph commits annual subscriptions as a distinct buyer-profile play — "a customer committing to a year of Luciel up-front is not the same buyer who needs a trial window" — with the cadence priced at 10× the monthly rate. The mathematical equivalence to "2 months free per year" is true (10 monthly bills' worth of price for 12 months of service ⇔ 2 free months) but the framing is a discount-play framing that reads against the §14 stance. The Pricing surface currently leans on the "2 months free" framing as the annual-card headline; the realignment is to lean on the one-bill-a-year framing instead, with the 10× anchor visible as a price calculation but not as the rhetorical hook.
**Section that raised it:** Pre-Journey-1 live-testing pause, 2026-05-20, during the partner walk of the live Pricing surface alongside the umbrella tier-realignment drift. Sub-concern of Pricing-page truth (`D-pricing-page-truth-2026-05-20`), separated out because the framing decision is a §14-doctrine decision — the Pricing surface is one implementation of it; future surfaces (an email upsell from monthly-to-annual, a sales call talk-track, an annual-renewal in-app prompt) inherit the same framing decision.
**Raised by:** Aryan (partner) on 2026-05-20, in the same direction-setting message. Decision locked in the partner clarification round: "Annual cadence — Stays. 'Pay yearly, billed once × 10'. Drop '2 months free' framing."
**Design claim:** CANONICAL_RECAP §14 "Annual cadence shape" paragraph commits annual as a different buyer-profile choice, not a discount-play. The current Pricing-surface framing ("2 months free per year") reads against that stance by leading with discount language. The realignment claim is to lift the §14 stance into the marketing surface verbatim: annual is "One bill a year, billed once at 10× the monthly rate" — the price is the same as 12× monthly minus 2 months' worth, but the framing is what-the-buyer-is-actually-committing-to (one decision, one bill), not what-they-are-saving.
**Repo state:** Defect in two places. (a) `Luciel-Website/src/pages/Pricing.tsx` annual-card copy — every "2 months free" string on every tier's annual card is replaced with "One bill a year" framing. (b) `Luciel/docs/CANONICAL_RECAP.md` §14 paragraph 2 ("Annual cadence shape") — the current language commits the one-bill-a-year framing in principle but the Pricing surface inherits the implementation-side "2 months free" from an earlier era; the §14 paragraph is correct as-is and does not need a doctrine change, only the website surface needs to catch up to it.
**Operational impact today:** Low — the annual-card framing has not converted any customer today (zero annual SKUs sold on the live wire). Impact is forward-looking: the first annual-cadence buyer reads the Pricing surface, and the framing they read becomes the framing they expect to see in the in-app annual-renewal prompt at month 12. Front-loading the one-bill-a-year framing today means the renewal-prompt surface (built later) can lean on the same framing without a customer-visible inconsistency.
**Owning roadmap step:** Step 30a.6 (Tier-hierarchy realignment) closing tag, paired with the four sibling drifts. Pass 3 of the realignment commit arc. Folded into the same `Pricing.tsx` edit as the trial-copy + Book-a-demo fixes.
**Resolution path:** Single-paragraph edit at `Luciel-Website/src/pages/Pricing.tsx` annual-card headline. Three string replacements (one per tier): "2 months free" → "One bill a year, billed once × 10". The 10× math is the same; the headline is what-the-buyer-commits-to instead of what-they-save. Add one vitest case at `Luciel-Website/src/pages/__tests__/Pricing.test.tsx` pinning the contract: the rendered Pricing surface contains no occurrence of the substring `"2 months free"`.
**Pattern E:** Pure copy fix at the website-surface layer. No backend touch. No schema change. No price change (the underlying Stripe Prices for annual cadence are unchanged; this is a marketing framing of the same 10× math). No regression risk to the monthly-card framing.
**Validation evidence:** Pending. Discovery evidence is the 2026-05-20 partner walk against the live Pricing surface.
